\subsection{Detailed Description}
Peripheral memory map for M\+K\+L25\+Z4. 

\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
1.\+8 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
2015-\/02-\/19 This header file implements peripheral memory map for M\+K\+L25\+Z4 processor. 
\end{DoxyDate}
